RESOLUTION2_NNP In_IN addition_NN to_TO the_DT inoculation_NN performed_VBD during_IN the_DT year_NN ,_, the_DT Veterinary_NNP Assistant_NNP Surgeons_NNP working_VBG in_IN the_DT mufassal_NN visited_VBD 20,594_CD villages_NNS and_CC treated_VBD 2,17,788_CD cases_NNS as_IN against_IN 18,494_CD villages_NNS visited_VBN and_CC 2,37,252_CD cases_NNS treated_VBN in_IN the_DT previous_JJ year_NN ._.
It_PRP is_VBZ satisfactory_JJ to_TO notice_VB that_IN the_DT cattle_NNS fairs_NN and_CC shows_VBZ continued_VBN to_TO be_VB attended_VBN by_IN the_DT departmental_JJ officers_NNS who_WP took_VBD the_DT opportunity_NN of_IN delivering_VBG lectures_NNS on_IN veterinary_JJ matters_NNS and_CC of_IN explaining_VBG to_TO the_DT people_NNS the_DT modern_JJ methods_NNS of_IN treatment_NN of_IN diseases_NNS and_CC of_IN the_DT care_NN ,_, management_NN and_CC upkeep_NN of_IN cattle_NNS ._.
This_DT is_VBZ essentially_RB necessary_JJ for_IN the_DT development_NN of_IN veterinary_JJ knowledge_NN among_IN cultivators_NNS who_WP are_VBP proverbially_RB conservative_JJ ._.
During_IN the_DT year_NN the_DT Veterinary_NNP Vaccine_NNP Section_NNP was_VBD opened_VBN on_IN a_DT permanent_JJ basis_NN replacing_VBG the_DT temporary_JJ vaccine_NN depot_NN ._.
This_DT section_NN is_VBZ equipped_VBN not_RB only_RB to_TO make_VB and_CC supply_VB goat_JJ tissue_NN vaccine_NN but_CC has_VBZ cold_VBN storage_NN sufficient_NN to_TO carry_VB a_DT stock_NN of_IN other_JJ sera_NN and_CC vaccines_NNS for_IN distribution_NN to_TO the_DT districts_NNS ._.
Arrangements_NNS for_IN carrying_VBG out_RP micros-_JJ copic_NN ,_, cultural_JJ and_CC biological_JJ tests_NNS also_RB exist_VBP in_IN this_DT section_NN ._.
It_PRP has_VBZ taken_VBN over_RP the_DT work_NN of_IN examination_NN of_IN slides_NNS and_CC specimens_NNS from_IN the_DT districts_NNS ,_, except_IN for_IN rabies_NNS work_VBP ,_, and_CC after_IN diagnosis_NN ,_, distributes_VBZ the_DT appropriate_JJ sera_NN or_CC vaccines_NNS ._.

The_DT history_NN of_IN this_DT report_NN starts_VBZ from_IN the_DT ``_`` Partition_NNP of_IN Bengal_NNP ''_'' ._.
Prior_RB to_TO the_DT partition_NN of_IN the_DT province_NN the_DT head_NN of_IN the_DT Department_NNP was_VBD the_DT Director_NNP ,_, having_VBG under_IN him_PRP the_DT Deputy_NNP Director_NNP ._.

At_IN the_DT time_NN of_IN partition_NN of_IN the_DT province_NN the_DT share_NN of_IN the_DT staff_NN that_WDT fell_VBD to_TO West_NNP Bengal_NNP consisted_VBD of_IN only_RB 8_CD Veterinary_JJ Inspectors_NNS and_CC 73_CD Veterinary_NNP Assistant_NNP Surgeons_NNP against_IN a_DT sanctioned_JJ cadre_NN of_IN 19_CD Veterinary_JJ Inspectors_NNS and_CC 110_CD Veterinary_NNP Assistant_NNP Surgeons_NNP ._.
